It is a moment of introspection, a moment of self that offers a quiet inner celebration of grace and soulful beauty. A simple whiff takes us away from the hum of the outside and brings us back “in”.</p>

<p>Matcha tea accord is infused with a creamy fig note, grounded by soft vetiver and textural cedar woods and uplifted by enticing bitter orange.<br />
<br />
Introverted and deep by nature, The Matcha 26 is a skin scent, something meant for, and only those individuals lucky enough to be very close to, the wearer. It carries a noble stillness. To us, it is a scented reminder of home, of welcomed solitude, and of all things familiar and treasured.</p></div><p class="reviewstrigger" style="font-size: smaller; color: #83a6c4">Read about this padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2326281" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Vintila R."/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1570569"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1570569.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Vintila R." style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2326281ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2326281" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.8); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1570569">Vintila R.</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-24">10/24/24 11:51</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I test this fragrance every time I pass by the Le Labo store. At this point, I have to say that I enjoy it more than I would like to admit. There are so many reasons why I shouldn't be contemplating a full bottle: It smells like a space (hotel lobby) or a shower product more than a personal perfume, it leans too masculine on my skin (that dry vetiver), I can't smell a straightforward tea (which I was expecting -based on the name-), the opening is too citrusy, the aromatic quality is sharp (I usually prefer more natural aromatics like the Aqua Allegorias from Guerlain), similar DNA of Santal 33 and other Le Labo products (I rather choose the mystery than the recognition), the price (of course). There are so many reasons why I shouldn't buy this expensive bottle, and here I am, making excuses to allow myself to do it. My responsible alter ego will probably stop me. Seriously, I think I would enjoy this more on a man. Carefree, dry and sweet, fresh and sexy!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="69731"comment_id="2326281"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Matcha-26-69731.html?ccid=2326281#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2320855" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Definitely more of a feminine scent but of course wear what you want.  Almost reminds me of green Turkish delight in a way. It's not photorealistic of anything just a delicious smooth and powder sugar coated sweet fig and tea-like scent.  But not too gourmand as it has enough depth with other notes not to smell edible.  I wish it had more sillage though it's very close to skin but can  still be smelled for several hours, and it takes a few sprays to really feel like it's noticeable. Possibly needing some sprays on clothes too. Which means you'll likely run out of such an expensive perfume if you wear it daily! But it may be worth it for such a beauty of a scent.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="69731"comment_id="2316058"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Matcha-26-69731.html?ccid=2316058#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2313736" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2313736" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="byrehoe"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1577248"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1577248.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="byrehoe" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Liis/Studied-69543.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.69543.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Studied"title="Studied"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2313736ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2313736" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.86); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1577248">byrehoe</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-12">10/12/24 17:42</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Dry, mineral green. Dehydrated fig latex, powdered moss, cedar sawdust. There’s bitter citrus rind – maybe a kaffir lime – for texture. I’m no a matcha expert and I know this isn’t photorealistic, but it still reads tealike to my nose. Maybe it's the impression of green tea, to a lifelong coffee drinker. This is clean, monotone, unisex. I get a “concrete petrichor” accord that almost echoes Baie 19. Sillage is mild, but longevity is solid. I can waft it for days in fabric. Years later and I keep coming back for more.  <br />
<br />
Mental Snapshot: A postwar laboratory, all concrete and block glass. The memory of tea, recalled through a boardroom of stern-faced scientists. Each atomises a clear distillate into their stainless steel teacup, and they contemplate the twenty-sixth iteration. While unpleasant to taste, it provides a pleasant aroma. <br />
<br />
tl;dr: brutalist tea ceremony 🏢🍵</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="69731"comment_id="2313736"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Matcha-26-69731.html?ccid=2313736#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2310219" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1460347">Scooty77</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-10">09/10/24 11:23</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>So, granted, I have the Dossier version of this, which isn't listed in this database, so I'm curious how far off it is to the real thing. However, I'm obsessed with this scent.  It's warm, powdery, green-ish, and a little sweet.  I buy a certain brand of matcha tea, and I swear, if I mixed this with some sort of cedary powder, it would smell just like this.  This isn't like anything I normally wear. It's even a little old-fashioned somehow. But it's cozy, creamy, and lovely. I'm not too fond of coconut in perfume, and this doesn't have that as a note, but I get a beautiful kiss of it somehow.  I will be purchasing the real thing and doing a comparison test for sure.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="69731"comment_id="2278151"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Matcha-26-69731.html?ccid=2278151#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2277807" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2277807" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Forelsket"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1455469"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1455469.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Forelsket" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2277807ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2277807" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.88); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1455469">Forelsket</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-10">09/10/24 04:58</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I had no expectation for this perfume, so the pleasure was even greater when I first sprayed it. It begins with a lovely fig, that turns very creamy within 10 seconds. It reminds me of Philosykos but creamier, very coconut-y (ironically, while there is coconut in Philosykos, there isn't any in Thé Matcha 26). <br />
<br />
I sprayed on a paper strip first and it becomes citrusy quite quickly, but on my skin I don't smell any citrus until much later on, it stays coconuty, creamy fig for a while. Then it becomes more woody, while retaining the creamy fig. It then reminds me faintly of an Abercrombie perfume I wore when I was 18, probably because of the vetiver. <br />
<br />
Cedar is present, it brings with it the citrus and it blends wonderfully with the creamy fig. I still can smell a faint coconut, I wonder from which note I get that.<br />
<br />
It definitely reminds me of Matcha, but rather a Matcha Latte, with coconut milk. It should have been named Matcha Latte 26, but it's not a gourmand scent so it could have been misleading. <br />
<br />
I sprayed it on my wrists and I can smell it without having to smell my wrists, so I'd say it performs slightly better than most skin scents, probably because of the blend of wood, citrus and fig. I get wiffs of the scent frequently, it's delightful.<br />
<br />
Le Labo describe it as quiet and reflective, but I find it rather energizing, especially on a grey, humid day. <br />
<br />
I'm really loving this scent, I'll edit this review if my opinion changes over time.<br />
<br />
EDIT 5th October: I bought the full bottle after falling in love with the sample. It's NOTHING like the sample, I'm hugely disappointed. Some say to let it sit, and the scent does change, but not in a good way: 2-3 weeks ago, I smelled basically nothing. Yesterday I tried it again and it smelled a bit more but so acidic and headache inducing. Miles away from the magic of the sample. I've reached out to Le Labo, I'll edit once I know more. Very disappointed.<br />
<br />
Sample: 9/10<br />
Full bottle: 1/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="69731"comment_id="2277807"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Matcha-26-69731.html?ccid=2277807#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2275127" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2275127" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="theboybmw"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2244383"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="theboybmw" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2275127ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2275127" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.74); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2244383">theboybmw</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-07">09/07/24 14:39</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I think everyone that says it doesn't smell like matcha has never smelled matcha before. Matcha has an astringent, sour note even in high end varieties that is only present when you smell it straight from the powder. This cologne is interesting because thanks to the citrus additions you get that astringent note at the same time as an almost menthol-y tea note, whereas in matcha powder you get one note before the other. <br />
<br />
All in all this fragrance smells like a drier, less synthetic Afternoon Swim.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="69731"comment_id="2275127"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Matcha-26-69731.html?ccid=2275127#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2273863" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It's not the strongest, but if you spray a decent amount, someone sitting next to you can smell it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="69731"comment_id="2258196"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Matcha-26-69731.html?ccid=2258196#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2258120" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2224652" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="montee"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1221166"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1221166.gif" class="comments-avatar"alt="montee" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Bond-No-9/Chinatown-1300.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.1300.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Chinatown"title="Chinatown"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2224652ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2224652" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.71); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1221166">montee</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-20">07/20/24 15:46</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Very round and classically built. Easygoing smell, though a little harsh on the opening.<br />
<br />
Coniferous naturals and woman-ly aromachemicals, vintage and kind of edgy smell… sounds about Le Labo. Designer-esque / made to smell decent and fashionable. Very mature smelling. Good longevity, moderate projection. What else is there here…. certainly doesn’t smell like Matcha and isn’t really niche-smelling. A little bit of this here and there blahblahblah....<br />
<br />
I tried to love Le Labo, but stuff like this just feels too conservative &amp; mainstream and thus not very interesting. Absolutely unjustifiable price. Wouldn’t make for a signature smell or anything distinctive for the matter. This isn’t anything new… if you don’t love Le Labo scents then you probably won’t love this either. I don’t dislike it though, 6.5/10.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="69731"comment_id="2224652"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Matcha-26-69731.html?ccid=2224652#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2222561" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2222561" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="StrangeTrails"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2138040"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2138040.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="StrangeTrails" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Atelier-Cologne/Santal-Carmin-25292.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.25292.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Santal Carmin"title="Santal Carmin"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2222561ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2222561" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.88); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2138040">StrangeTrails</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-18">07/18/24 13:07</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I love this perfume.<br />
<br />
As others have mentioned, this isn't really a "matcha" fragrance as a photorealistic scent, it's more of an artistic interpretation.  It opens creamy and sweet from the fig, the orange cuts through but it's more of a bitter citrus peel orange, balancing out the sweetness from the fig. Cedar is there and warm in the background, with the vetiver in this pulling a real green, clean and grassy vetiver rather than a velvety vetiver - I think the vetiver is what is giving this that "soapy" clean vibe. Though it's not listed here, one of the most prominent topnotes I get from this is haygrass. This perfume to me smells like a barn full of freshly cut and bundled alfalfa, drying in bales. It's very nostalgic of my farm upbringing, and for that reason I love it. <br />
<br />
Here and there as the scent evolves, the green notes mellow into a waft of a cup of green tea, but again it's more of an artistic idea of the scent of drifting green tea than it is a photorealistic matcha. It's distinct from a jasmine green tea though, so I suppose matcha fits. <br />
<br />
This is definitely a "skin scent" on me, low projection and sillage. You have to be very close to smell it. And it doesn't last as long as other Le Labo fragrances from me either, but I like it enough to forgive these indiscretions. I don't buy a full bottle though because for the crazy insane price they want it's simply not got a good enough performance. I pick up decants of this instead. It's an excellent spring or hot weather fragrance (currently wearing it in 38° C weather as I write this review), and it leans equally unisex for me - I'd love to smell this on a man on a date night, as it's unusual and not overpowering, and very classy, but I equally enjoy wearing it myself.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; Now, I tried this on my friend and was amazed by how different it smells on her. In her skin this is pure orange and matcha but after a few hours develops into an almost sandalwood scent but sweeter.<br />
This feels femenine but mature</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="69731"comment_id="2213627"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Matcha-26-69731.html?ccid=2213627#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2211258" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2211258" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="stidal"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2117272"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2117272.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="stidal" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Boka/Zelen-87722.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.87722.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Zelen"title="Zelen"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2211258ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2211258" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.84); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2117272">stidal</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-07">07/07/24 15:52</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>As many have already said, this one doesn't really scream matcha, despite the name. It's kind of confusing. It's a creamy, sort of powdery fig; but not powdery in the way that iris or violet notes tend to be? I think that this note is what's meant to be matcha. As someone who makes their own matcha pretty often though, it doesn't have that green, umami, tea-like smell that the actual powder does. It evokes matcha without actually smelling like it. It's like the shell or ghost of matcha. I don't know, I'm just rambling at this point. In any case, I do like it quite a bit. Pretty good staying power, projects pretty well, too. Great unisex scent! Love smelling this on pretty much anyone. <br />
<br />
Side note: if you're on the hunt for a photorealistic matcha, give Rag &amp; Bone's Genmaicha a shot!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="69731"comment_id="2211258"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Matcha-26-69731.html?ccid=2211258#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2209619" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2209619" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="cheleine"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1349744"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1349744.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="cheleine" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Diptyque/Eau-Duelle-Eau-de-Toilette-9241.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.9241.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Eau Duelle Eau de Toilette"title="Eau Duelle Eau de Toilette"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2209619ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2209619" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.81); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1349744">cheleine</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-05">07/05/24 22:57</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The only offering from Le Labo I can confidently say that was love at first sniff for me.<br />
Nothing else really spoke to me like this one.<br />
It is a scent that made me smile.<br />
There is something very smooth and soft and uplifting about its composition. <br />
I don’t really understand the comments saying they don’t get the matcha note. <br />
To me this smells like a very light and frothy matcha latte but it’s done in an elegant way, it’s not a gourmand, it’s a signature worthy scent that could work for any occasion really as a natural scent of your skin. <br />
There is a milky facet to this perfume, probably coming from the fig note. It’s a wellness scent. Very soothing, happy, anti-depressing. I really adore it and will probably get a bottle but I’m not sure about the performance.<br />
<br />
Edit: It smells like a romanticised version of matcha tea. What most people wished matcha smelled like. Because what the actual tea powder smells like is quite bitter, harsh and green. Here we have a soft, sweet, smooth and pleasant blend accompanied by many other notes (most prominently fig, vetiver, citrus, musk). To me (because I just had it this morning) it smells like a matcha latte drink you’d expect from Starbucks. <br />
It feels very milky and creamy but it’s done in an elevated way and as I said, it’s not gourmand forward. <br />
It’s a cool and zen scent and it will probably become my new signature but as I said the performance is not the best. I wish the sillage was a little better and it probably has ISO because I stop smelling it quickly but others keep smelling it on me. <br />
I’m in love but for that price I’d want it to perform better. <br />
I still got a bottle though.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="69731"comment_id="2209619"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Matcha-26-69731.html?ccid=2209619#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2209409" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; To me it has the super sexy, jeans and a pristine white t-shirt vibe that CKOne has, but with the sophistication, longevity and depth of Le Labo. Super clean, a bit soapy and very athletic. She goes to pilates, steams and showers BEFORE the office. Definitely a day time scent. She's in bed by 10pm after a 12 step skin care routine.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="69731"comment_id="2209409"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Matcha-26-69731.html?ccid=2209409#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2206827" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2206827" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="TBonetheFella"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1710835"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1710835.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="TBonetheFella" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Etat-Libre-d-Orange/Tom-of-Finland-4524.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.4524.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Tom of Finland"title="Tom of Finland"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2206827ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2206827" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.9); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1710835">TBonetheFella</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-03">07/03/24 06:04</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The professional fig.<br />
<br />
As soon as I spray this on I am hit in the face an overdose by green, yet juicy fig, bitter &amp; effervescent orange, and powdery matcha. Not overly sweet like most figs can be, but zingy, tart, and refreshing. Then as it dries down, the orange begins to blend into a super clean, woody cedar/vetiver mix, giving way to the classic woody fig, but with the added twist of a slight green and powdery backbone. <br />
<br />
This is NOT a matcha/tea forward fragrance, this is a zingy, woody/fig. If you go into this really wanting that, you’ll prolly walk away pretty disappointed. That being said, where other popular figs like “Philosykos” by Diptyque or “Debaser” by DS &amp; Durga are green, sweet, fruity, and fun; this one is woody, fruity, zingy, and professional. Truthfully, I wish there was more of a focus on matcha than it ended up having, but no use crying over spilled milk. I really enjoy this fragrance, and I think 99% of people will as well, especially since it’s not super heavy and thick. Very well done, and very versatile. A solid fig fragrance, and would be good for someone who typically doesn’t like sweet fragrances. A solid like.<br />
<br />
Fair good performance with moderate to intimate projection. <br />
<br />
8.5/10. <br />
<br />
Song vibe - Casio by Jungle</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="69731"comment_id="2206827"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Matcha-26-69731.html?ccid=2206827#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2204582" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2175271">emmamarie444</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-23">06/23/24 17:52</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This scent is very complex and goes through many different seasons as you wear it. At first spray, I get a very strong musk and citrus smell that I actually don't like at first. I wish Le Labo could try to dial back that initial intensity but after 30-60 minutes the sharpness starts to wears off and the softer scents of fig, vetiver and green tea start to come forward and balance out the scent and it is quite powdery/milky. At that point, I absolutely love how this smells like soft clean skin or bed sheets. It's a very intimate and lived in scent that only people close to you can really smell and I love it for that. It starts off a lot more unisex and slightly masculine, but after 1-2 hours it's quite warm nurturing and feminine. This is my absolutely favourite to wear fresh out of the shower and is my daily go to. In some ways, it almost smells like a rich hotel spa. It's very soothing and introverted as le labo describes. I wouldn't say this is a very "matcha" like smell but it's the essence of greenery, nature, skin, woods that makes it so.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="69731"comment_id="2197532"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Matcha-26-69731.html?ccid=2197532#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2186258" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Sniff" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2145768ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2145768" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.72); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1878218">Scratch &amp; Sniff</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-04">05/04/24 14:55</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I really wanted to love this scent, but I just cannot bring myself to do it after repeated attempts.  Le Labo fragrances are very hit or miss, and I guess Thé Matcha 26 just doesn’t “match-a” my taste or skin chemistry.  On me, this smells immediately spicy and there’s something extremely abrasive about it, which just becomes more and more off-putting the longer it lingers.<br />
 <br />
With its list of notes, I should, in theory, adore this.  I love fig-based fragrances, green earthy notes, and I like the scent of matcha.  But I’ve tried this fragrance multiple times, and all I get is woods and spice.  It smells like spicy Christmas…whatever that means, I’m not even entirely sure TBH.  But I am sure that I need to give up on this one.<br />
<br />
Le Labo describes this fragrance as “introverted and deep by nature, Thé Matcha 26 is a skin scent, something meant for, and only those individuals lucky enough to be very close to, the wearer.”  To which I ask, skin scent?  FOR WHOM, exactly?!  This ain’t no skin scent - this is a spice bomb that holds its wearer captive at gunpoint and teabags your nostrils like it’s conducting a water-boarding interrogation.  Alright, Le Labo, I’ll tell you what you want to know, just make the spiciness stop!<br />
 <br />
PS – for those who don’t know, it’s Thé Matcha, not The Matcha ("thé" as in the French word for "tea"). While it might be pretentious to dole out language lessons, we are still talking about the French here.<br />
 <br />
In five words or less: This matcha isn’t a match.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="69731"comment_id="2145768"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Matcha-26-69731.html?ccid=2145768#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2144480" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2144480" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="SophiaG"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1227475"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="SophiaG" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Lancome/Idole-L-Intense-62333.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.62333.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Idôle L'Intense"title="Idôle L'Intense"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2144480ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2144480" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.89); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1227475">SophiaG</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-03">05/03/24 09:49</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I do not like Le Labo fragrances - I've never found one that I would buy, and I'm really not a fan of smelling them on other people either. I'm sure it's my nose, because I cannot smell a single note that people are describing in the comments. <br />
<br />
I will say that at first spray, there is a distinct creaminess and an intriguing dry vetiver underneath it all that made me hopeful that it could be one that works on my skin, but alas - it gets sour as time passes and the combination of that and the earthy vetiver is very reminiscent of body odor.<br />
<br />
There is a distinct Le Labo DNA that comes across as hot plastic. With Santal 33, it's plastic mixed with pickle, and with Thé Matcha it's plasticky sweat. I think this brand and me will just never get along, but I still think it's worth testing if there's a fragrance counter near you.<br />
<br />
Edit: I found a fragrance that reminds me of this but does it so much better. Avocado Toast by DSH perfumes is an incredibly creamy fragrance that has hints of greeness and earthy grain notes. To me, it's a sister to Thé Matcha (not the same, but comparable) without the grating synthetics.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="69731"comment_id="2144480"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Matcha-26-69731.html?ccid=2144480#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2142658" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1484705">salaryman</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-13">04/13/24 17:18</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This fragrance starts out with a very strong orange and cedar smell. Once it dries down, the matcha note starts popping out. It’s a very green and earthy kind of smell that’s combined with the near-overwhelming sweetness of the bitter oranges at the same time. There is an awkward phase at the beginning where I can’t really tell whether I like it or not, but it doesn’t take very long for all the different scents to start balancing out nicely and smell like a real sweet matcha!<br />
<br />
I was a bit confused at how I couldn’t smell the fig at all, but after reading a bit more into the fragrance I realised they’re using the scent from the fig leaves and not the fig itself! Which is interesting. I think it works out well for this perfume. <br />
<br />
The sillage is pretty similar to Noir 29, except the moderateness only lasts for about an hour instead of two before it shifts to sitting very close to the skin. The longevity is also moderate.<br />
<br />
While I have been looking for a green scent to add to my collection, The Matcha 26 is too earthy on me, so I likely won’t be getting a full bottle for this one, but I’ll make good use out of what remains of my tester!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; Opening with citrusy matcha fades quickly.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="69731"comment_id="2109178"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Matcha-26-69731.html?ccid=2109178#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2107860" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I drink matcha daily and have experimented with different grades. I'm sorry, there's no matcha here. Nor do I think of matcha as being particularly fragrant to begin with. But this is a wonderful fragrance. I am a fan of creamy, lactonic fig as opposed to fresh, green fig. This feels like a modern composition to me. When I smelled this, I thought maybe I should give up my dream of finding a decadent signature fragrance, as regulations and trends seem to be phasing out that once-abundant style. Maybe I would embrace wearing a gentle skin scent and a new era. This perfume is perfectly modern, a quiet cocoon for the wearer.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="69731"comment_id="2086876"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Matcha-26-69731.html?ccid=2086876#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2085447" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Thé Noir is one of my all time favourite fragrances, so I had to give this a try and I wasn’t disappointed. A creamy sweet fig note, juicy but not overpowering orange, fresh greenery, and the slightest, subtle smokiness from vetiver. <br />
<br />
I said that I love Thé Noir because it’s sweet, fresh and smoky all at the same time. So is Thé Matcha, but in a totally different way. No, you don’t get a lot of matcha, that note fleetingly hangs around in background, but I don’t even care.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="69731"comment_id="2071927"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Matcha-26-69731.html?ccid=2071927#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2071794" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2071794" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="wannabeconnoisseur"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1935900"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1935900.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="wannabeconnoisseur" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2071794ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2071794" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.72); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1935900">wannabeconnoisseur</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-02-23">02/23/24 13:32</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Bitter orange strikes first, rich and juicy. Deeper and livelier than typical citruses. Against the cedar, the warm orange is amplified and creates a soft, inviting tea accord. Far from matcha, but the same comfort of creamy tea is here; something cozy and relaxing, and natural. The dry cedar binds everything together. Vetiver is absolutely present and I can feel its green and sparkling character. Something about it is almost spicy, but less pepper and more ginger, or cinnamon. I'm surprised more people haven't perceived it this way! The bitterness keeps the orange out of sticky sweet territory. Instead, this is soft and approachable, and relaxed enough for daily wear. A remarkably fresh but grounded vibe.<br />
<br />
Very, very fig. Really, it's the entire tree, not just the fruit. I suspect they put 'matcha' in the name only to take advantage of the skyrocketing popularity of matcha. Something in this doesn't sit well on my skin, and I get an unpleasant sourness after a few hours. But my skin turns everything earthier, so I had to jettison this. <br />
<br />
Years back, there was a candle at Target, called Leave Your Worries Behind, from Happy Place. Its scent was fig tree. This smells almost exactly like that candle; and that's not a bad thing. I must have bought that candle ten times before it was discontinued.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="69731"comment_id="2071794"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Matcha-26-69731.html?ccid=2071794#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2070746" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="69731"comment_id="2070746"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Matcha-26-69731.html?ccid=2070746#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2069822" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2069822" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="smellysmellz83"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2012408"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="smellysmellz83" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2069822ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2069822" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.8); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2012408">smellysmellz83</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-02-21">02/21/24 15:53</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>As a tea connoisseur, I was extremely excited to try this fragrance. I grew up drinking green teas and eating matcha-flavored products. As an adult, I stock my cabinet with a wide selection of green teas: matcha, genmaicha, hojicha, etc. When I sprayed this scent, I was hoping for a kind of distilled "eau de green tea", but instead, I was overwhelmed with a strong, almost sickeningly sweet smell that burned my nostrils (the fig, I think). It was sharp, pungent, and reminiscent of overripe flowers/fruit, or perhaps of wet wicker furniture left to mold. It somehow reminded me of plastic or play-doh. These notes lasted for 1–2 hours. After that, the dry down revealed more of the matcha notes, and when I closed my eyes and concentrated, I could imagine that I was inhaling the scent of a hot cup of matcha in my hands. However, there was also a cloying sweetness reminiscent of Nishane's Wulong Cha (the fig?) as well as a wood note reminiscent of Santal 33 (the cedar?). These notes for me were undesirable, and the play-doh or plastic impression never entirely went away. Overall, the dry down was not offensive, but it also wasn't particularly pleasant. This perfume lasted at least 8 hours on me.<br />
<br />
When I think of matcha, I think of clean, grassy warmth. The appeal of a high-quality cup of matcha or green tea is in its simplicity. Because I strongly disliked the fermented/overripe impression, and because I found the sweet and woody base notes distracting, I'd rate this a 4/10.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; I get more a woody, fig and slightly creamy scent. I don't really get matcha. <br />

I say go for it. I'm talking to the REAL matcha lovers, not the basic kind that think you can only have it with oat milk. This is a beautiful, fresh, clean matcha perfume. Nothing in your face.<br />
<br />
It's being out on the country on a nice chilly day, no wind, just perfect. Sitting around an open flame, your better half putting a pot of water to boil while you just watch.. It's ready, he grabs an enamel steel mug and pours in some hot water. He opens up a packet of green tea, adds honey and lets it steep while he mixes matcha in a separate mug. Grabs ice from his YETI cooler, puts some in a mason jar, pours in the green tea, then matcha, a bit of cinnamon, a lice of orange, and stirs. He hands it to you, along with fresh cut figs, and a kiss. "Thank you baby" You say to him, smiling in admiration.<br />
<br />
That's what it smells like to me. Fresh figs &amp; an iced matcha green tea with honey, an orange slice and cinnamon. On a bright chilly day. It's refreshing, energetic but warm at the same time. I love it alone during the day, if I go out at night, I do layer with coconut. (It performs better, in my opinion) Turning it into an iced matcha coconut latte with cinnamon. But much more sophisticated, cozy, and incredibly sexy! One of my favorites from Le Labo. padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1867647">oneyoungtreesprout</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-10-17">10/17/23 15:12</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>one of my most expensive perfumes, but i can justify it because i love it so much. i smell the fig sometimes when i sniff the nozzle, but not really on the skin. the first spray is bright green floral and citrus with a slight creamy sweetness. this is where i smell the fig the most before it disappears completely. i actually don't get "airy" at all; if anything, there is a deep velvety musk (other commenters have noted this is probably iso e), on which the refreshing matcha-orange scents blend on top of. it dries down on me and the brightness turns slightly sour and the cream powdery scent dries into something more sweet and woody, like if old books had a fruity quality instead of a dustiness. i have also sampled santal 33 by le labo, and while i understand the comparison, to me, the matcha 26 is far more modern and leans softer and more feminine to some while santal 33 is harsher, louder, and truly unisex. the smell dissipates very quickly outdoors, so don't waste this scent spraying it on outer layers of clothes. wear it sparingly and directly on the skin, and let the scent transform over the day, so that when someone is within arms length of you they will pick up the most subtly complicated sweet scent.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; It opens quite green, herbal and woody but dries down to a figgy, softly spiced dry down. I feel like this is a good white t-shirt scent for daily/office wear. It is like a soapier, more minimal version of Parisian Musc by Matiere Premiere. And a softer, less spicy, more daytime appropriate little sister to my beloved The Noir 29. It captures the savoury nature of matcha, smells like a woody almost salty musk, in the same wheelhouse as Eau Papier by Diptyque, and suitable for the same occasions. If this scent was a colour it would be green, not as vivid as matcha green but a pale peppermint green.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="69731"comment_id="1944649"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Matcha-26-69731.html?ccid=1944649#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1936854" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1908036" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="sabertooth_salem"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1310673"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1310673.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="sabertooth_salem" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1908036ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1908036" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.75); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1310673">sabertooth_salem</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-08-21">08/21/23 16:59</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>In my opinion, Le Labo's "signature" is in their blending -- camouflaging the notes their fragrances are named after in skillful or unexpected ways, rather than showcasing them front and center. This can sometimes be misleading to those who are not familiar with the house. Santal is a blast of dill, labdanum is powdery civet, patchouli becomes Memphis bbq and so on...<br />
<br />
The Matcha 26 is no different, but it is absolutely lovely. Opening is a clean floral green tea which settles into a creamy, sweet fig and cedar base. Like other reviewers have mentioned, there definitely seems to be some Iso E here even though it is not listed. You can smell it very clearly after a few hours -- cozy &amp; airy. <br />
<br />
If I could go back in time, I would definitely purchase this over Santal 33 as it is overall smoother, creamier, and more refined and luxurious.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1906572" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="auderpop"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1816568"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="auderpop" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1906572ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1906572" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.7); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1816568">auderpop</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-08-19">08/19/23 20:21</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I smelled this in store without knowing the notes first. It smelled nice enough on paper, so I tried it on skin.<br />
<br />
I've been looking for a fig fragrance. Philosykos was was beautiful, but too green for it to feel like it was for me. Thé Matcha is so creamy, and I like that it's more of a skin scent. My nose tends to be sensitive, and I headache easily with most fragrances, tending to spray my fragrances for four sprays and nothing more. My boyfriend can spray his cologne strength fragrance, and I'll smell it from across the room. I'm a fan of cedar base notes.<br />
<br />
I get creamy fig for the first half of the fragrance, and the bitter orange helps balance out how strong the fig is on initial spray. I don't get matcha until about halfway in, where it's still not the main event, but best supporting actor. I get the touches of creamy earthy bitterness of the matcha that balance out the fig. I think most wouldn't classify this as a sweet fragrance, and I don't like sweet fragrances at all, but there's just a touch of sweetness from the fig that is perfect for me.<br />
<br />
I tested this in store at noon, and am writing at 8:30 PM. I still smell the fig when I press my nose to skin, and though gone now, I got whiffs on cinnamon once the 6 hour mark hit. This fragrance really has multiple stages of development on me, and I can't wait to smell it again.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="69731"comment_id="1906572"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Matcha-26-69731.html?ccid=1906572#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1901439" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1901439" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Venetian Tangerine"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1730000"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1730000.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Venetian Tangerine" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1901439ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1901439" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.84); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1730000">Venetian Tangerine</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-08-13">08/13/23 16:08</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Don't believe the olfactory pyramid, this is one of the best blended creamy perfumes you'll find.<br />
<br />
It holds together different and almost opposing facets: an interesting bitter orange opening (with a hardly perceptible green accord of matcha tea laid on it) and a very creamy wood base.<br />
Some might resemble this creaminess to some of the milkiest sandalwoods out there (TF santal blush), but it does go much deeper (and more natural) than that, with a deliciousness that reminds you of the fruity tobacco base of other le labo's The Noir. Other than sweet tobacco and buttery sandalwood the accord smells simply creamy in the most light whipped-cream sense, never too gourmand but very much in a segue from the dribbling fruit core: a gorgeous lactonic fig.<br />
This delicious cental fruity accord is often used by le labo with different inflections: nightly and sexy in The Noir, fresh and elegant in Bergamote and properly ripe and creamy here.<br />
Describing it as a pure fig would be far from the truth (nothing like the photorealistic one in Philosikos-diptyque).<br />
Rather, it's that irresistible le labo fruit blend, here rendered as a very pulpy late summer fruit concoction: definite ripe peach, hints of delicious plums/prunes (+ cherries maybe?) and a good dose of rich juicy figs.<br />
<br />
The pulpy fruit core - which is never overpowering (see: pulp byredo) - magically connects and envelops the deep creamy finish with the citrus opening, for a mix which is energizing and comforting at once, but most of all simply exquisite.<br />
<br />
Worth a try, regardless of your taste.<br />
<br />
9.1/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="69731"comment_id="1901439"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Matcha-26-69731.html?ccid=1901439#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1900090" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Goetz Dark Rum, but then it takes a more herbal, grounded turn. they both have that clean soapiness to me, with a slight hint at citrus. padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1172778">ievaid</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-08-07">08/07/23 06:46</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>last time i sampled a matcha fragrance it left me wishing for more astringency and more androgyny. thé matcha 26 by le labo has both in spades. what it doesn't have, regrettably, is a lot of matcha. <br />
<br />
the citrus and the bitter-herbal vetiver create an impression that reminds me of slightly oversteeped green tea with lemon peel, but i don't get the grounded earthiness that is particular to matcha. though fleeting, i think replica's matcha meditation did a better job in conveying that specific matcha character. i also don't get a lot of the sweetness from the fig; to me this is downright green and woody and masculine-leaning. i like the cedar base, though: it's warm and comfortingly solid, a soft heart underneath a sharp exterior.<br />
<br />
another reviewer pointed out that this smells like iso e super, and that was the eureka moment for me: that's exactly it! that sour, almost brutalist note that somehow reminds me a little of old electronics, which is nearly a weird enough scent association to make me enjoy it — but at the end of the day i'd still rather wear something else, unless i'm in a rather ascetic and/or masculine mood.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex;
