Sometimes it my skin which drinks-up fragrance, so I made sure to spray this on my clothes. I sprayed 8 times and in the first hour my boyfriend commented that I smelt really nice, but after that it had become a close skin scent and it fades away unnoticed into oblivion. Such a shame, as Matcha 26 has all of the hallmarks to be my signature scent - it’s bamboo-woody, gently figgy without being too fruity, it’s not pickley like 33 or 29, it has a soft-spice-sophistication, the matcha is comforting as it encapsulates the warmth of the frothy green cup itself, it’s just perfectly zen-like, it’s atmospheric and unassuming like an innocent summers day from an idyllic childhood.<br />
If Le Labo ever makes The Matcha 26 intense version, I’d have found my most perfect scent.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="69731"comment_id="1854332"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Matcha-26-69731.html?ccid=1854332#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1853942" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1850813" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="domesticangel"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1736269"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1736269.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="domesticangel" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1850813ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1850813" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.77); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1736269">domesticangel</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-06-06">06/06/23 21:09</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>when I got the chance to visit le labo in san fran I was initially only interested in making a beeline towards another 13 (which I did and I loved, but that’s neither here nor there), but when I smelled the dry down of thé matcha on paper, I was instantly captivated. this is such a beautiful scent—I agree with other reviewers that it’s fairly linear, but there’s also a lot of complexity brewing underneath that consistency if that makes sense.<br />
<br />
I personally do get a lot of the matcha smell—another user mentioned high quality matcha bringing in a sort of umami note, and I totally get that. this opens on the greener end, but once this dries down on my skin and ESPECIALLY on my clothes, an almost savory undertone begins to develop. the sharpness of the citrus and vetiver is so beautifully cradled by warm and creamy notes, and it really does start to take on that intimate warm skin quality.<br />
<br />
it surprising to me that this is classified as a skin scent—for me, this projects far, lasts an entire day on skin, and has so far lasted an entire WEEK on a hoodie I wore with it. I’m fairly pleased with the performance!<br />
<br />
I think the more heady, umami quality pushes this just barely into not a safe blind buy territory. I almost hesitate to say this because I don’t want to scare others off from what is really a lovely fragrance, but something about this almost evokes…mustard? to my nose at least! key word being EVOKES—I can’t say it actually smells like mustard to me, but rather has a similar quality of being simultaneously tart, warm, and a little naturally sweet. I’m wondering if it’s just because of those sharper notes pulled down by something warmer and creamier, and that’s the first association my brain made for whatever reason, haha! but anyway, do keep in mind this is a LOVE review—I definitely don’t want to scare anyone off! just try before you buy, is all.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; I think most people are familiar with matcha being green, bitter, earthy, etc. but good matcha such as Uji Hikari Cultivar matcha can smell of Unami, floral, citrusy, smooth, and sweet. I personally believe Le Labo did an amazing job capturing a good ceremonial grade matcha scent. The first 10-20min you get a good burst of citrus. The fig ads a smooth floral and green, but light sweetness. The backbone is woody but not over powering! Overall Matcha 26 is a light and comfy scent that embodies the spirit of a good Uji matcha that makes me feel calm and grounded. Although it is a lighter scent, it last about 6-7 hours.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="69731"comment_id="1793260"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Matcha-26-69731.html?ccid=1793260#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1793047" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I would say this is a lighter version of another fig scent I adore, Figfever by Hermetica Paris that is heavier and for wintertime.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1697913">Salandria828</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-03-25">03/25/23 17:24</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I’m coming around to really liking, and maybe even loving this fragrance. Like several other reviewers, I smell almost nothing but fig on my skin, and that led to a sense of initial disappointment with it. I really wanted the Matcha tea to reign supreme, or at least be as present as the fig to make it more interesting and in keeping with its description on the website. That said, I do like the way this fragrance dries down on me rather quickly into a creamy yet bright-but-not-sharp figgy richness. (Is that due to a soupçon of the bitter orange and cedar that I’m maybe perceiving? 🤔)<br />
<br />
Now that I’ve adjusted my expectations to something far less complex and mysterious than it claims to be, I’ve come to appreciate the fact that Thé Matcha 26 performs well on my skin with its solid longevity, linear performance (which is a plus in my opinion, as long as I like what I’m smelling!) and sillage that leans more toward intimate. I’m now considering adding this to my small regular fragrance lineup. A little goes a long way for me,  so I’m getting a good, long run out of the sample I ordered from the company, and I find myself reaching for it again and again and liking it more each time.<br />
<br />
If you’re a lover of figs, I’d recommend giving this a try. In spite of Le Labo’s vibe that borders on the embarrassingly pretentious, they did manage to do justice to this lovely fruit by rendering it into a pleasing, if not straightforward, skin scent. Furthermore, the sticker shock is thankfully softened by the fact that a tiny spritz packs a good wallop, in the very best of ways.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1491812">abuk</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-02-17">02/17/23 10:41</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>My recent trip to the Le Labo store in Brooklyn was a memorable experience. As I explored the fragrances, one particular scent caught my attention and blew me away. The Matcha 26 was so refreshing and captivating that I decided to purchase a tester on the spot, and a week later, I invested in a full-size bottle. <br />
<br />
While some consider this a spring/fall scent, I believe it's versatile enough to wear year round. On it's own, the fragrance's fig, green tea, and cedar elements shine brilliantly, creating a fragrance that's perfect for fall, summer, and spring. During the colder months, the woody notes stand out, but what I love to do is layer it with Santal 33 to create a warmer interpretation. Blending the leathery/sandalwood notes from Santal 33 with the bright, bitter orange and delicate, creamy fig notes from The Matcha, creates a scent fit for a crisp winter.<br />
<br />
Despite this scent's sillage being labeled as intimate, I've received compliments from people standing a few feet away. It's a beautifully subtle and versatile fragrance that never seems to overwhelm and my girlfriend loves it just as much as I do.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/614231">jassca99</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-12-21">12/21/22 03:33</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I smell a burst of fig, citrus and fresh matcha, which isn’t too bitter but slightly green, in the opening which I love. Then it dries down to mostly bright cedar with remnants of the first mentioned notes. I honestly don’t get the Santal 33 and smell-alike comparisons. This is very woody but still not the pickled wood chip that people get in Santal 33, because there are fruity, aromatic facets preventing that. The fig is more fresh-fruity in the beginning to me, maybe with the help of the citrus, but it does become a little creamy. Never being harsh, they’re soft around the edges while still adding freshness. Very calming.<br />
<br />
Projection quickly closes in as you wear, but a little more than intimate. Like the lower range of moderate. Somewhere in between. This also has moderate longevity to me at the moment. I do feel like it would get lost in the summer heat since it’s not as bright, but I’ll have to wait til next summer to confirm since it is winter now. However, I see this being perfect for spring and early fall. The Matcha 26 leans a little more feminine but can pass as unisex in my opinion.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="69731"comment_id="1714008"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Matcha-26-69731.html?ccid=1714008#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1708160" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; There's a fresh, woodsy greenness to it-- not the decidedly powdery, bitter, earthy, matcha tea-greenness. Every now and again I pick up a coconutty aspect, which is often the case with fig-forward compositions IMO. It reminds me a lot of Libertine's Eros Fig, minus the more sensual, warm, honeyed base notes. So I consider this to be a cooler and more aloof fig offering, with pretty good lasting power, and therefore pretty much on-brand for Le Labo overall (minus the naming mishap).</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1503389">mizur</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-09-28">09/28/22 21:56</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Creamy citrusy matcha tea… nice, very nice.<br />
<br />
As a personal preference, I wished the fig had been dialed up just a smidge… still, this is a deliciously clean scent.<br />
<br />
The Matcha Tea is soft and airy… the Bitter Orange is not bitter at all, just tangy and citrusy… the Fig, although distant, is sweet and lactonic… and the Cedar is quaintly enveloping the whole fragrance… the rest of the notes are not distinguishable on their own, but surely encompassing the rest.<br />
<br />
Quite similar to Imagination from Louis Vuitton just with matcha instead of black tea.<br />
<br />
Longevity is around ten hours… projection is moderate the firsts couple of hours, then it becomes intimate… completely unisex, and wearable in spring and summer, preferably during daytime.<br />
<br />
Again… very nice creamy citrusy matcha tea perfume.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="69731"comment_id="1655115"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Matcha-26-69731.html?ccid=1655115#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1654952" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;     <div class="grid-x grid-padding-x grid-margin-y" style="position: relative; padding: 0 0.25rem 0 0.25rem;">
                            <div id="parent1421578" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1421578" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="17seyed"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1165604"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1165604.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="17seyed" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1421578ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck6x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1421578" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.74); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1165604">17seyed</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2021-10-03">10/03/21 15:14</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I've been wearing my sample for a few days. The Matcha 26 isn't terribly complex but it's small assortment of detectable notes are blended well together.<br />
<br />
It opens with a huge dose of tea and something mildly citrusy and sweet. The citrus fades away quickly after 10 minutes, but the tea scent is preserved and is intertwined with a crisp floral accord; this is my favorite stage of the fragrance. It remains like that for a couple of hours and is where the fragrance really shines. You have a herbal and green facet with the matcha that is elevated even more with the floral notes, but then brought back down to earth with the vetiver. This stage reminds me very SLIGHTLY of Bal d'Afrique.<br />
<br />
The late dry down is dominated by fig and sandalwood. Closest I can describe relative to other Le Labo fragrances would be a mix of Santal 33 and The Noir 29, but with the former's leathery and "pickle" notes, and without the latter's smokey notes; all with a tiny splash of Another 13.<br />
<br />
I'm not the biggest fan of tea notes when they get too earthy or too rich, so I truly enjoy the balanced and light direction Le Labo took with this release.<br />
<br />
The biggest downside is, of course, the performance. It lasts quite a long time but the projection is almost non-existent.<br />
<br />
Kinda useless to wear outdoors, but it can make for a fantastic choice if you want a soothing fragrance to relax at home with.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="69731"comment_id="1421578"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Matcha-26-69731.html?ccid=1421578#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1956910" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1956910" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="spaceybailey"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1800427"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1800427.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="spaceybailey" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1956910ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1956910" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.84); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1800427">spaceybailey</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-10-20">10/20/23 12:57</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>If you're a MATCHA lover like me, debating whether or not you should buy this perfume. I say go for it. I'm talking to the REAL matcha lovers, not the basic kind that think you can only have it with oat milk. This is a beautiful, fresh, clean matcha perfume. Nothing in your face.<br />
<br />
It's being out on the country on a nice chilly day, no wind, just perfect. Sitting around an open flame, your better half putting a pot of water to boil while you just watch.. It's ready, he grabs an enamel steel mug and pours in some hot water. He opens up a packet of green tea, adds honey and lets it steep while he mixes matcha in a separate mug. Grabs ice from his YETI cooler, puts some in a mason jar, pours in the green tea, then matcha, a bit of cinnamon, a lice of orange, and stirs. He hands it to you, along with fresh cut figs, and a kiss. "Thank you baby" You say to him, smiling in admiration.<br />
<br />
That's what it smells like to me. Fresh figs &amp; an iced matcha green tea with honey, an orange slice and cinnamon. On a bright chilly day. It's refreshing, energetic but warm at the same time. I love it alone during the day, if I go out at night, I do layer with coconut. (It performs better, in my opinion) Turning it into an iced matcha coconut latte with cinnamon. But much more sophisticated, cozy, and incredibly sexy! One of my favorites from Le Labo. BISOUS</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="69731"comment_id="1956910"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Matcha-26-69731.html?ccid=1956910#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1486571" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1486571" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="gemma_ni"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1306852"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1306852.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="gemma_ni" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Frederic-Malle/Carnal-Flower-1024.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.1024.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Carnal Flower"title="Carnal Flower"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1486571ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1486571" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.89); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1306852">gemma_ni</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-01-19">01/19/22 12:22</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I think the name of a fragrance should be an introduction to how you would IMAGINE a scent. The bitterness comes from the citrus skin, the sweetness comes from a lactonic note, and the grassy feeling comes from the vetiver. Nothing is matcha but everything reminds me what matcha tastes like. Bitter and herbaceous when taking the first sip, but it leaves a sweet and fresh trace when you swallow it.<br />
<br />
Thé Noir 29, on the other hand, is deep and smokey, with a gourmand dry fruit touch. I've smelled many tea fragrances that actually smell like mate, whereas matcha effuses a young, light-weight, and herbal aroma, which is a completely different olfactive impression from mate.<br />
<br />
If scent had a color, Thé Matcha 26 is a light wash of muted wasabi green. It opens with crisp citrus, which is reminiscent of Bergamot 22 if you smelled it from a blotter. After a few minutes, the fig-sesame accord floats to the rim of your "teacup". The nuttiness is an interesting take of the fig, quite unusual among many fig-dominated fragrances. So, the performance of the first 10 minutes is more like a cologne. But with the scent developing on the skin, the creamy matcha latte accord appears and it is indeed long-lasting. It brings me back to the culture I grew up in. A culture where tea is served in a simple way, without syrup, whipped cream, or any Starbucks toppings.<br />
<br />
Even if "matcha" is a marketing jargon or an attempt to cater to Asian aesthetics, I totally buy it. From the purchase in October last year, I have been reaching this fragrance the most among my collection. This is beyond falling in love at first sight. This is a commitment.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="69731"comment_id="1486571"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Matcha-26-69731.html?ccid=1486571#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1435559" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1435559" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Birnam_Wood"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1061235"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1061235.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Birnam_Wood" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1435559ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1435559" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.83); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1061235">Birnam_Wood</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2021-10-27">10/27/21 11:09</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>-<br />
The naming methodology of Le Labo is simple: <br />
<br />
if a certain note is in the name, then you most definitely will <b>NOT</b> find it on the first try. Or the second.<br />
<br />
Le Labo's latest release <b>THÉ MATCHA 26</b> also follows the rule: I guarantee you, it has NOTHING to do with matcha, rather, it's a <b>crowd-pleasing fruity fragrance</b>, but not those run-of-the-mill brain-dead cheapies. <i>(NOT smell very expensive either, and not worth the exorbitant price, as ususal)</i><br />
<br />
<b>Main Notes</b><br />
Fig, Mango, subtle maltose syrup<br />
<br />
<b>Smells Good?</b> 7.6/10 <b>Smells Interesting?</b> 6.5/10<br />
<br />
<b>Scent Description</b><br />
<br />
It opens with <b>fresh figs</b> tainted by somewhat soapy citrus, also edged with a slight minty coolness (this can't be the so-called "matcha", can it?).<br />
<br />
Then the watery fig swiftly gets rid of citrusy notes, and slides into the arms of Le Labo's trademark  <b>"mango"</b> accord, which never appears in their note pyramids: this is not the scent of juicy fruit pulp, but an uncut, intact, <b>fully-ripe-but-not-overly-so mango skin</b>. It's rich and soft, in the same vein as THÉ NOIR 29.<br />
<br />
A creamy hint from base ooze up —— this subtle <b>creamy-maltose syrup tone</b> gave the mango a golden brown hue, but never overwhelms it. At some point a granular sugar sweetness is exposed, but fortunately not too much. <br />
<br />
The perfume changes little up to this point, it simply soft down and disappears.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="69731"comment_id="1435559"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Matcha-26-69731.html?ccid=1435559#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1655115" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1655115" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="mizur"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1503389"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1503389.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="mizur" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/M-Micallef/Sensual-40563.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.40563.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Sensual"title="Sensual"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1655115ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1655115" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.85); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1503389">mizur</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-09-28">09/28/22 21:56</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Creamy citrusy matcha tea… nice, very nice.<br />
<br />
As a personal preference, I wished the fig had been dialed up just a smidge… still, this is a deliciously clean scent.<br />
<br />
The Matcha Tea is soft and airy… the Bitter Orange is not bitter at all, just tangy and citrusy… the Fig, although distant, is sweet and lactonic… and the Cedar is quaintly enveloping the whole fragrance… the rest of the notes are not distinguishable on their own, but surely encompassing the rest.<br />
<br />
Quite similar to Imagination from Louis Vuitton just with matcha instead of black tea.<br />
<br />
Longevity is around ten hours… projection is moderate the firsts couple of hours, then it becomes intimate… completely unisex, and wearable in spring and summer, preferably during daytime.<br />
<br />
Again… very nice creamy citrusy matcha tea perfume.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="69731"comment_id="1655115"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Matcha-26-69731.html?ccid=1655115#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="69731" sentiment="positive"></reviews-infinity>

Sniff"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1878218"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1878218.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Scratch &amp; Sniff" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2145768ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2145768" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.73); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1878218">Scratch &amp; Sniff</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-04">05/04/24 14:55</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I really wanted to love this scent, but I just cannot bring myself to do it after repeated attempts.  Le Labo fragrances are very hit or miss, and I guess Thé Matcha 26 just doesn’t “match-a” my taste or skin chemistry.  On me, this smells immediately spicy and there’s something extremely abrasive about it, which just becomes more and more off-putting the longer it lingers.<br />
 <br />
With its list of notes, I should, in theory, adore this.  I love fig-based fragrances, green earthy notes, and I like the scent of matcha.  But I’ve tried this fragrance multiple times, and all I get is woods and spice.  It smells like spicy Christmas…whatever that means, I’m not even entirely sure TBH.  But I am sure that I need to give up on this one.<br />
<br />
Le Labo describes this fragrance as “introverted and deep by nature, Thé Matcha 26 is a skin scent, something meant for, and only those individuals lucky enough to be very close to, the wearer.”  To which I ask, skin scent?  FOR WHOM, exactly?!  This ain’t no skin scent - this is a spice bomb that holds its wearer captive at gunpoint and teabags your nostrils like it’s conducting a water-boarding interrogation.  Alright, Le Labo, I’ll tell you what you want to know, just make the spiciness stop!<br />
 <br />
PS – for those who don’t know, it’s Thé Matcha, not The Matcha ("thé" as in the French word for "tea"). While it might be pretentious to dole out language lessons, we are still talking about the French here.<br />
 <br />
In five words or less: This matcha isn’t a match.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="69731"comment_id="2145768"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Matcha-26-69731.html?ccid=2145768#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1421992" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;
